bur ba thams cad nges par dor ba'i mtshan nyid dang chos kyi dbyings so sor thob cing mngon par shes pa lnga dang ye shes mkhyen pas sangs rgyas kyis yongs su thob pa'i phyir chos thams cad kyi sgor blta bar bya'o// o~M sha Sha sa ha/ rnam pa thams cad kyi mchog dang ldan pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes rnam par dag pa rnam par 'byed par byed pa'o zhes so// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi sgo rnam par nges pa'o// de nas rigs thams cad kyi gsang ba'i cho ga rgyas par gyur pa ni/ sngon bzhin nges par byas nas ni// phyogs kun mnyam pa nyid bsgoms nas// ri rab chen po gru bzhi pa// rin chen kun gyis rnam par brgyan// de yi steng du rdo rje che// de yi steng du pad+ma gzhag // 'dab ma brgyad pa ches bkra ba// rnal 'byor gnas zhes rnam par bshad// dbang po gnyis ni snyoms 'jug pa// yongs su rdzogs par bdag nyid kyis// sangs rgyas thams cad nyid bsgoms na// de nas bskal pa'i mthar thug gnas// sangs rgyas kun gyi phyag rgya che// 'od zer gsal ba'i dkyil 'khor can// rnal 'byor thams cad bsgom par bya// mnyam med sangs rgyas kun dang mtshungs// b+ha ga chen po rnal 'byor che// rnal 'byor pa gnas mi zad pa// sangs rgyas kun bdag bsgoms nas ni// sangs rgyas kun dang mtshungs par 'gyur// khams gsum pa yi rgyal srid che// sems can kun la thams cad du// gang tshe rnal 'byor pas bsgoms na// de tshe dngos grub lag na gnas// rang bzhin gyis ni 'od gsal chos// gdod nas dag cing ma 'dres pa// gang tshe ye shes mthong ba ni// de yi tshe na dag par 'gyur// sangs rgyas thams cad mdor bsdus pa// sna tshogs las kyi sbyor ba yis// gang tshe rnal 'byor pas bsgoms na// sna tshogs las ni byed par 'gyur// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi phyag rgya chen po'i ye shes so// // 'khor los sgyur ba rgyal po che// kun mchog sa yi dbang phyug ni// rdo rje sbyor bas bsgoms na ni// mnyam med 'khor los sgyur ba mtshungs// gzi brjid phung po phyag rgya che// legs par mnyam par gzhag pa bsgom// 'bar ba'i phreng bas 'khrugs shing mdzes// pad+ma rA ga mtshungs pa'i 'od// rdo rje'i sbyor bas bsgoms nas ni// rang nyid gzi brjid phung por 'gyur// gdugs dkar rgyal ba'i gtsug tor gyi// phyag rgya chen po bsgoms na ni// 'od zer gsal ba'i sbyor ba yis// sems can dag pa nyid du 'gyur// rnam par gsal ba'i gtsug tor rgya// ral gri 'bar ba'i 'od kyis 'khrugs// zag pa med pa'i sbyor ba yis// mnyam med gsal ba'i gtsug tor mtshungs// rgyal ba'i gtsug tor phyag rgya che// legs par mnyam par gzhag pas bsgom// rgyal ba'i gtsug tor sbyor ba yis// de yi rnam pa'i spyod yul 'gyur// rdo rje dam tshig ye shes che// legs par mnyam par gzhag pas bsgom// kun tu bzang po sogs gzugs kyis// mnyam med rdo rje sems dpa' mtshungs// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor dbus gnas pa// rdo rje sems dpa' sems dpa' che// byang chub sems dang mtshungs pa'i 'od// gtsug tor lnga ldan stobs po che// rdo rje'i sbyor bas bsgoms pa yis// rdo rje sems dpa' 'dra bar 'gyur// rdo rje rgyal po'i phyag rgya che// don dam par ni bsgoms na ni// 'gro ba thams cad 'gugs byed na// skye bo gzhan lta smos ci dgos// rdo rje chags pa'i phyag rgya che// legs par mnyam par gzhag pa bsgom// skye dgu thams cad chags 'gyur na// bud med gzhan lta smos ci dgos// rdo rje legs pa'i phyag rgya che// dam pa'i don du bsgom par bya// legs so ba ni rab gsol bas// bud med thams cad tshim par byed// byang chub kyi sems kyi phyag rgya'i ye shes so// // rdo rje rin chen phyag rgya che// 'bar ba'i phreng bas 'khrugs pa'i 'od// dpral ba'i phyogs su gnas pa bsgom// de yis dar thod dbang bskur thob// rdo rje gzi brjid phyag rgya che// nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor mtshungs pa'i 'od// snying gar gnas pa bsgom par bya// kun mkhyen ye shes ster bar byed// rin chen tog gi phyag rgya che// legs par mnyam par gzhag pas bsgom// sbyin pa'i pha rol phyin pa mchog // sgrub po dam pas rdzogs par byed// rdo rje bzhad pa phyag rgya che// legs par mnyam par gzhag pas bsgom// rdo rje bzhad pa ltar gyur te// de ni skye dgu dga' byed 'gyur// dbang bskur ba'i phyag rgya'i ye shes so// // pad+ma bde chen pad+ma la// dag pa'i chos ni mnyam gzhag pas// dam pa'i don du bsgom par bya// mnyam med rdo rje chos dang mtshungs// shes rab ye shes rdo rje rno// bsgoms pas de ni rdo rje 'chang // shes rab pha rol phyin dag pa// stong nyid sbyor bas bsgoms na ni// dam pa'i don du bsgom bya de// mnyam med 'jam dbyangs dang ni mtshungs// rdo rje rgyu yi phyag rgya che// legs par mnyam par gzhag bsgoms nas// chos kyi 'khor lo kun mchog rtse// mdor bsdus nas ni de yis bskor// rdo rje smra ba'i phyag rgya che// dam pa'i don du bsgoms nas ni// rdo rje bzlas pa'i nus pa yis// ldem po'i ngag ni de yis 'chad// chos kyi phyag rgya'i ye shes so// // rdo rje las kyi phyag rgya che// dam pa'i don du bsgoms na ni// kun nas kun nas rang nyid kyis// rdo rje las ni byed par 'gyur// rdo rje bsrung ba byams pa che// rdo rje chos zhes grags pa ste// chos kyi sbyor bas bsgoms na ni// rdo rje bsrung ba dang mtshungs 'gyur// rdo rje gnod sbyin brtson 'grus che// khro bo chen po stobs po che// dam pa'i don gyis bsgom par bya// rdo rje gnod sbyin dang mtshungs 'gyur// rdo rje khu tshur phyag rgya che// lus ngag yid kyis de bzhin du// rdo rje'i sbyor bas bsgoms na ni// rdo rje khu tshur 'dzin par 'gyur// las kyi phyag rgya'i ye shes so// // sgeg mos mngon par dga' ba ster// phreng ba yang ni dbang bskur ba// glu mas mdzes pa'i sgra dbyangs byed// gar mas rdzu 'phrul thob par 'gyur// dri mas bzang po'i dri yin te// me tog byang chub yan lag nyid// sgron mas mtha' dag gsal ba'o// bdug pas bdug pa dag la brtson// lcags kyus dbang phyug 'gugs byed na// skye bo gzhan lta smos ci dgos// zhags pas dbang po 'ching 'gyur na// gdug pa'i sems can smos ci dgos// lcags sgrog gis ni 'phrog byed dang // tshangs sogs dbang phyug chen po'ang 'ching // 'bebs pas thams cad 'bebs 'gyur na// dman pa'i mi dag smos ci dgos// 'di nyid kyi ni sbyor ba yis// chos kyi yi ge mchog gi ni// phyag rgya'i ye shes rab sbyor bas// sbyar te myur du bsgrub par bya// 'di yi sbyor ba shes par bya// phyag rgya'i 'khor lo khyad par du// spyi gtsug snying ga rkang pa'i bar// yi ge yis ni yongs gang par// gzugs brnyan gcig gi go 'phang gyur// sems rtse gcig 'gyur bsam gtan gyis// sa la rab gnas pad+ma ni// dbang chen gyi ni gnas zhes bshad// dbang po gnyis ni mtshungs sbyor bas// dbang phyug kyang ni bsgrub par bya// dbang chen dag ni gru bzhi pa// dbang chen gyi ni las su bshad// chu ni zlum par shes par bya// pad+ma'i mtshan mas rnam par mtshan// zhi bar byed pa'i las dang ldan// zhi ba'i don du de bshad do// me ni gru gsum shes par bya// sum mdo yi ni gnas su gnas// dbang du bya ba bsgrub don du// pad+ma rA ga 'dra ba'i 'od// mngon spyod la ni brtson 'grus che// rlung gi dkyil 'khor brjod bya ste// ral gri yi ni phyag rgya'i dbyibs// dbyar gyi sprin dang mtshungs pa'i 'od// ser dang dkar dang de bzhin dmar// nag po yang ni khyad par du// dang po'i dkyil 'khor tshul gyis ni// tha ma'i bar du rab tu brtag // dang po rdo rje rab tu gzhag // de yi rjes su rin chen te// pad+ma dang ni las rnal 'byor// grub pa'i go 'phang rim par bshad// phyag rgya thams cad kyi ye shes so// // de nas bcom ldan 'das rtag pas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi phyag rgya'i ye shes bka' stsal pa/ gnyis dang gnyis su med pas yongs su dag pas chos thams cad rnam par grol ba'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// rtag pa yongs su dag pas chos thams cad zhi ba dang mtha' dang mtha' med pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// zad pa'i sgo dang zad pa'i mtha' dang zad pa'i mur thug pa dang ldan pas chos thams cad zad pa dang / 'dod chags dang bral ba'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// mnyam pa nyid kyi mtha' rnam par dag pas chos thams cad la skur pa mi 'debs pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// mig lnga la yang dag par 'das pas chos thams cad nam mkha'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// sems can thams cad nam mkha'i dbyings nyid kyi phyir chos thams cad nam mkha'i rang bzhin gyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// chos kyi dbyings su yang dag par 'du ba nyid kyi phyir/ chos thams cad dbyer mi phyed pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// byang chub kyi sems dang tha mi dad pas chos thams cad byang chub kyi sems kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// chos kyi dbyings mi phyed pa'i mtshan nyid yin pas chos thams cad chos kyi dbyings kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// ngo bo nyid med pas chos thams cad stong pa nyid kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// 'tshe ba med pas chos thams cad bdag med pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// skad cig ma nyid pas chos thams cad mi rtag pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// skye ba dang rga ba dang 'chi ba'i mtha' dang ldan pas chos thams cad sdug bsngal gyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// sngon gyi mtha' dang phyi ma'i mtha' de bzhin nyid pas chos thams cad de bzhin nyid kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// gdod ma nas yongs su dag pas chos thams cad yang dag pa'i mtha'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// 'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas mnyam pa nyid pas chos thams cad chen po stong pa nyid kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// spros pa'i dmigs pa rnam par bral bas chos thams cad mtshan ma med pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// re ba thams cad las rnam par grol bas chos thams cad smon pa med pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid kyi mtshan nyid kyis na chos thams cad mi rtag pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// phung po lnga yongs su 'dus pa'i mtshan nyid kyis na chos thams cad sdug bsngal gyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// rang bzhin gyis bdag med pas chos thams cad bdag med pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// shin tu mi g.yo ba'i phyir chos thams cad zhi ba'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// don dam pa'i bden pa yang dag par 'du ba'i phyir chos thams cad bden pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// 'tsho ba rnam par mi gnas pa'i phyir chos thams chos thams cad ji lta ba bzhin gyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// 'jal ba'i dbang du byed pa dang dbang du bya ba med pa'i phyir chos thams cad sgro 'dogs pa med pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// byed pa pos byas pa'i phyir chos thams cad 'jig pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// rang bzhin gyis ma byung ba'i phyir chos thams cad 'byung ba med pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// rang bzhin gyis ma rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// mngon par 'du byed pa thams cad med pa'i phyir chos thams cad las kyi rnam par smin pa med pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// skye ba dang gnas pa las rnam par grol ba'i phyir chos thams cad 'dus ma byas pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// nam mkha' dang khyad par med pa'i phyir chos thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// mtshan nyid gcig pa'i phyir chos thams cad gzugs dang / tshor ba dang / 'du shes dang / 'du byed dang / rnam par shes pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// snying po med pa'i phyir chos thams cad phung po'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// snying po dang bcas pa med pa'i phyir chos thams cad khams dang skye mched kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sku dang mnyam pa nyid thob pas chos thams cad khams dang skye mched kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// mtha' gcig tu 'jig rten gyi lam rnam par dag pa'i phyir chos thams cad 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// lha rjes su byed pa'i phyir chos thams cad phyag rgya chen po'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// mtha' gcig tu chos la phan 'dogs pa'i phyir chos thams cad chos kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// thams cad kyi las sna tshogs byed pa'i rgyas rgyas btab pa dang // gsang sngags kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa dang / phyag rgya'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa dang / dkyil 'khor gyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa dang / mnyam pa nyid kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa dang / rdo rje ye shes kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa dang / ye shes thams cad kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa dang / me long lta bu'i ye shes kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa dang / mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa dang / so sor rtog pa'i ye shes kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa dang / bya ba grub pa'i ye shes kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa dang / chos thams cad chos kyi dbyings rnam par dag pa'i ye shes kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes kyi phyag rgya'o// muH/ 'jam dpal phyag rgya'i tshig 'di dag ni mi mnyam pa dang mnyam pa'i ye shes kyi tshig de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis byin gyis brlabs pa'i tshig thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes yongs su rdzogs par byed pa theg pa chen po'i tshig ste/ 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dang / byang chub kyi phyag rgya nyid kyi phyag rgya'i tshig gang gis/ phyag rgya'i tshig 'di rnams kyis kyang chos kyi phung po brgyad khri bzhi stong skyed par byed do// sems can thams cad kyi sems kyi rgyud la phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// a a~M aHA~M/ sngags pas phyag rgya 'di lta bus rgyas btab na de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi phyag rgya yang dag par 'du'o// hU~M/ myur du ma skyes pa'i chos rnams la bzod pa thob par 'gyur ro// kha~M/ de nas da ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sbyor ba thams cad kyi gsang ba chen po'i phyag rgya'i ye shes su gyur pa ni/ snying gi dbus su rtag bsgom bya// pad+ma chen po 'dab brgyad pa// 'bar ba'i phreng bas 'khrigs pa'i 'od// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor dbus son par// de yi steng du rtag bsgom pa// yi ge yi ni gtso bo mchog // thog ma tha ma med zhi ba// kha ba ba mo'i 'od 'dra 'od// dpa' bo kun+da zla ltar dkar// nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor ltar 'od gsal// zhi ba'i chos kyi rang bzhin sku// kun mkhyen ye shes kyis gang ba// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi gsang // ra sA ya na dang mtshungs mchog // kha yig mkha' 'drar shes par bya// thig le nA das rnam par spras// gsang ba chen po mchog tu mdzes// thog ma tha ma med pa'i bdag // de yi steng du 'od zer che// 'bar ba'i phreng ba 'khrugs pa'i 'od// rdo rje rdo rje lta bur gnas// spyi bor rtse mo lnga dang ldan// de yi steng du rtag bsams pa// yi ge mchog gi go 'phang ngo // man ngag mchog las shes bya ste// gzhan du na ni nga mi smra// sangs rgyas mkhas pa thams cad kyis// mdor bsdus nas ni 'di gsungs so// rnam par grol ba gsum thob nas// thob 'gyur 'di ni gzhan du min// lce ni rkan la sbyar bar bya// sna yi rtse mor yi ge hU~M// dbang po gnyis ni snyoms 'jug pas// phyag rgya'i go 'phang tshig gis ni// shes rab ldan pas rang sems bsgom// snang ba med cing spros med pa// shin tu mchog tu phrar shes bya// khyab bdag bsod nams ye shes dngos// bsam bya bsam gtan brtson byas te// mig dang sgron ma'i 'od bzhin du// ra yig 'bar ba dang ldan pa// mgrin pa 'bad pas gcum nas ni// dkar po ser po sngon po'i 'od// dmar po yang ni bdag gis spro// 'bar ba 'di dag 'bad pa yis// 'di dag yang dag nyer mtshon bya// snying gar gsal bar byas nas su// de bzhin thams cad spyi bor song // gnas de las ni 'thon nas kyang // dbang po thams cad dgang bar byas// de las 'thon nas 'jig rten ni// mtshungs par kun nas thams cad du// slar yang de ru 'ongs nas ni// de ni 'jug par rab tu bsam// yid kyis de ltar bsgoms na ni// rang nyid 'khor los sgyur lta bur// dbang po gnyis ni rab sbyor bas// legs par mnyam par gzhag pas bsgom// dbang po lngas ni dmigs nas yang // mi rnams lus ni dag par 'gyur// ji snyed bud med yon tan dang // ldan pa kun du gnas pa ni// bkug nas bcug ste bcings nas su// dbang du bya ste bsgrub par bya// de rnams lhan cig yongs brten nas// sngags pa mchog gi dngos grub thob// gsang ba mchog tu dgyes pa na/ shes rab pha rol phyin pa ste// zhi ba'i chos kyi rim pa mchog // shin tu mnyam par gzhag pas bsgom// rdo rje sems dpa'i dngos grub gang // de 'grub gzhan lta smos ci dgos// mchog ni rtag par shes par bya// bar mas phun sum tshogs pa ste// stong pa nyid dang mtshan med mchog // smon pa med pa zhes su grags// chos kun bdag med pa yi mchog // kun mkhyen ye shes rdzogs par byed// sa bcu yi ni stobs dag gis// pha rol phyin pa thams cad thob// rdo rje sems dpa' mchog bsgoms nas// rdo rje sems dpa' 'dra bar 'gyur// de nyid 'di ni bcud kyis len// gnyis su med pa'i ye shes mchog // theg chen mchog tu yid 'ong ba// stong nyid bsgom pa'i bdag nyid can// gnyis su med pa'i ye shes mchog // gang gis rtag tu sgom byed na// de yang rdo rje 'dzin rgyal po// yon tan mchog las skyes par 'gyur// rgyan rnams kun gyis rnam par brgyan// bud med lus ngag yid sbyor bas// yongs reg A liM ga tsum+bas// mchog gi dngos grub thob par 'gyur// bud med kha dog ljang gu gang // rgyan rnams kun gyis rnam par brgyan// de tshe de ni sngags pas bsten// mnyam med gsang ba'i ye shes mtshungs// bud med gang zhig kha dog dkar// pad+ma'i 'dab ma 'dra ba'i 'od// de dang lhan cig sngags pas bsdad// dam pa'i dngos grub thob par 'gyur// bu mo gang zhig kha dog dmar// ut+pa la yi rgyan 'chang ma// sngags pas de dang lhan cig gnas// shes rab pha rol phyin mtshungs 'gyur// bud med in dra nI la mtshungs// gsang ba rdo rje rjes su sbyor// rig 'dzin rnams kyi rgyal po ni// stobs chen grub par de 'gyur ro// gsang chen ma ra ka ta mtshungs// gang gis rtag tu bsten pa ni// de yang rdo rje 'dzin rgyal po// myur du gsang ba'i dam par 'gyur// bud med pad+ma rA ga 'dra// rgyan rnams kun gyis rnam par brgyan// dbang po gnyis ni snyoms 'jug pas// rdo rje 'dzin ma lta bur bsgrub// sangs rgyas kun dang mnyam sbyor ba// gnyis su med pa'i ye shes mchog // bsam pas rtag tu bsgom pa ni// mnyam med sangs rgyas kun dang mtshungs// dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bzhi// mchog gis gnas kyis bsgoms na ni// rnal 'byor mchog gis mi ring bar// rdo rje 'dzin pa lta bur 'gyur// yang dag spong ba rnam pa bzhi// legs par mnyam par gzhag pa bsgom// dbang po gnyis ni snyoms 'jug pas// mnyam med 'jig rten dbang phyug mtshungs// so so yang dag rig pa bzhi// shin tu mnyam gzhag du gyur nas nye bar gnas// phyag rgya gcig pa'i lha mo che// rol cing g.yo ba'i zhal mnga' ba// sgeg pa la sogs nyams dang ldan// rol cing snang ba'i gar mdzad pa// sangs rgyas spyan ni 'grub par 'gyur// mig gi phyag rgya rab tu sbyar// mig gi phyag rgya 'di shin tu// 'jig rten gsum yang gar byed do// sangs rgyas spyan gyi phyag rgya'i sgrub pa'i thabs so// // chu yi dkyil 'khor dgyes pa na// 'khor chen po'i dbus su ni// rnal 'byor dbang phyug chen mo mchog // phyag bzhi spyan ni gsum pa dang // ral pa'i cod pan dag gis brgyan// 'dam bu mda' rgyu'i mdog ltar dkar// dpa' ba la sogs nyams gnyer can gyi sgrub pa'i thabs so// // nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor rdo rje ldan// rdo rje'i phreng bas yongs su bskor// gzi brjid dkyil 'khor kun nas dkris// der gnas // de yi thugs kar rdo rje che// 'bar ba'i phreng ba 'khrigs pa'i 'od// de yi 'bar ba lcags sgrog gi// rnam pa rdo rje'i mtshan mas mtshan// nges par phyung nas de dag kun// chos dbyings mnyam dang mi 'jig rten skyong dang klu rnams kyang // rang gi gnas nas bskyod nas ni// grub pa kun gyi dngos grub ni// dngos grub 'gugs par 'dod pa yis// thams cad gus pas sbyin par byed// bud med gzugs kyis spyod yul yang // de srid de yi 'od zer bsgom// rnal 'byor ye shes kyis rab sprul// sngags ni/ oM tsa le tsu le tsun+de swA hA/ 'di yi sngags kyi mchog gtso bo// sangs rgyas kun gyis mchod pa po// mtshungs pa med pa'i dngos grub ster// lha dang lha min bcas pas mchod// 'di yi sdig kun 'dzad byed cing // phun sum tshogs kun rab stsol mdzad// pad+ma'i phyag rgya yang dag ldan// sangs rgyas nyid kyang ster byed pa'o// skul byed ma'i sgrub pa'i thabs so// // gsang ba mchog gi dgyes pa na// thams cad bdag nyid rtag tu bzhugs// sangs rgyas kun bdag dgyes pa ni// rdo rje sems dpa' bde ba'i mchog // 'di ni rang byung bcom ldan 'das// gcig pu nyid ni lhag pa'i lha// sangs rgyas kun dang mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro ma yi dra ba sdom// 'dod chags med cing chags bral med// dbu mar dmigs par mi 'gyur ro// bud med kun gyi sgyu ma'i rgya// 'di ni gnyis med theg pa'i mchog // sgyu ma dag ni thams cad las// bud med sgyu ma khyad par 'phags// nus pa yi ni rang bzhin gyis// rang bzhin nyid kyis de grub bo// 'jig rten gsum gyi bud med 'dis// bkur bar bya ba 'os pa yin// ngan sbyong rnams kyis kyang 'grub ste// rnyed pa kun dang bde dang spro// thams cad bud med sgyu mas 'grub// rang gi ngo bo yongs bsgyur ba// sna tshogs sgyu ma'i phyag rgya 'di// shes rab pha rol phyin mar bshad// kun la sna tshogs phyag rgya ni// kun la sna tshogs sdom pa yis// sangs rgyas kun dang mnyam par sbyor// stong pa nyid kyis de nyid bskul// kun la kun nas thams cad du// rnam kun kun tshe rang nyid kyis// sangs rgyas thams cad brtan dang g.yo// thams cad dngos po rang nyid 'gyur// sems dang sems can ting 'dzin dang // byang chub spyod pa sna tshogs nyid// sa dang pha rol phyin spyod pa// dbang nyid du yang de bshad do// bdud dang bdud las rgyal ba nyid// sangs rgyas rdo rje de bzhin gshegs// thog ma ral gri 'dzin rgyal po// 'khor lo de bzhin 'khor lo 'dzin// 'jig rten gsum rgyal nyid dang ni// 'di rnams kyi yang rigs nyid 'gyur// de nyid chags dang chags bral ba// 'dod dang thar pa ru yang 'gyur// dus gsum dang ni srid gsum mchog // 'jig rten gsum dang khams gsum pa// brtan pa thams cad de nyid de// rnam pa sna tshogs nyid du 'gyur// g.yo ba kun nas sna tshogs pa// thams cad du ni de 'gyur ro// de la sogs pa sna tshogs mchog // chos dbyings mnyam dang mi mnyam pa// nam mkha'i khams kyi mtha' klas pa// dngos po kun du de 'gyur ro// de nyid bcom ldan rnal 'byor te// gcig pu nyid ni lhag pa'i lha// nam mkha' kun gyi skabs na dpal// rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs// dpal ldan sgyu ma chen mo 'chang // rnam snang rtag pa thams cad du// rnal 'byor dbang phyug gtso chen khyab// sangs rgyas 'khor lo can mi bskyod// che dang rin chen 'byung stobs che// tshe dpag med pa kun nas mchog // don yod sna tshogs mdzad pa dang // rdo rje sems dpa' blta na sdug // dgug pa mchog gi sbyor ba dang // legs par mdzad pa de nyid yin// rin chen sgron ma de bzhin tog // rdo rje bzhad pa snang ba che// rdo rje chos dang rno ba che// rgyu dang smra mchog bdud rtsi dang // las dang go cha gnod sbyin che// khu tshur de bzhin gshegs pa kun// de nyid bcom ldan rnal 'byor 'di// rdo rje sems dpa' stobs po che// rdo rje hU~M mdzad hU~M mdzad dang // rta mgrin zhes ni rnam par grags// he ru ka dpal rdo rje che// mchog gi dbang phyug gshin rje gshed// khro bo gzegs ma snang ba che// rdo rje me ni 'od chen po// gzugs rnams kyi ni mchog gcig pu// ting nge 'dzin las dbang sgyur ma// shes rab pha rol phyin mchog gtso// sa dang pha rol phyin pa stobs// tshangs pa'i gnas pa chen po bzhi// dbang ni mchog tu 'bar ba dang // dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bzhi// dbang po rnams dang stobs rnams dang // rjes dran drug por gyur pa gang // bsgom par bya bar rab tu gnas// de nyid bcom ldan gcig pu ste// byang chub yan lag bdun btags pa// mtha' gcig yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur// sum cu rtsa gnyis mchog gi mtshan// 'jig rten 'das pa'i lam po che// 'phags lam yan lag brgyad btags pa// stobs bcu yi ni bcu pa nyid// sangs rgyas chos kyi bdag nyid gnas// byang chub phyogs kyi tshos chen po// rnam par dbye ba sum cu bdun// mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms 'jug ni// dgu la gnas par gyur pa dang // bsdu ba'i dngos po chen po bzhis// sems can bsdu bas sdud pa dang // so so yang dag rig pa bzhi// de bzhin bsrung ba mi mnga' ba// skal ba chen po'i mi 'jigs pa// mchog tu gyur pa nyid dang ni// bsam gtan gzugs med bzhi phrag gnyis// tshad med pa yang de bzhin no// byang chub sems kyi spyod pa gtso// bden pa bzhi ni ston pa po// kun nas nyon mongs rnam par byang // zag bcas zag pa med pa'i mchog // de nyid bcom ldan rnal 'byor te// dbang phyug mchog gi dbang phyug dang // skye dgu'i bdag po skye dgu'i sgra yis rnam dgod pa// 'jig rten tha snyad tshul du rtogs// de tshe lus sogs dbye ba yis// sa rnams kyis ni yongs su brtags// sku ni sprul pa nyid du 'gyur// longs spyod rdzogs pa yang dag brnyes// rtogs par bya ba las kyi sku// rnam pa gsum du'ang dbye bar bya// de nyid bcom ldan rnal 'byor te// byang chub sems ni 'od gsal ba// kun du 'od kyi sa chen po// nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor gzi brjid ldan// pa brtan pa'i sbyor ba yis// rdo rje zhes ni yongs su bsgrags// lnga pa rin chen 'od ces bya// dbang bskur bar ni rab tu gnas// drug pa pad+mo 'chang zhes bya// pad bzhin rab tu rnam par snang // rang dpe dang bral zhes bya// dpe rnams thams cad rab 'jug pa// bcu pa shes rab 'od ces bya// sangs rgyas sa ni bla na med// bcu gcig kun mkhyen nyid ces bya// sa chen po ni 'od gsal ba// bcu gnyis so sor bdag rig pa// rnal 'byor ye shes yongs rdzogs nyid// sa chen po ni 'di dag rnams// sangs rgyas rnams kyis don dam du// sangs rgyas dang ni sangs rgyas chos// rnal 'byor ye shes gang brjod pa// thams 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis bcom ldan 'das thog ma dang tha ma med pa chos kyi 'khor lo chen po bskor ba rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po la gsol ba btab pa/ de nas bcom ldan 'das rdo rje rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen pos de dag gis gsol ba btab pa'i tshig gi de ma thag nyid du de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mnyam pa nyid du dmigs pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la mnyam par bzhengs te/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// 'jam dpal de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi theg pa chen po mngon par rtogs pa zhes bya ba'i dkyil 'khor chen po yod do zhes ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la btsugs te thal mo sbyar nas btud de 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bstan du gsol/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang / thabs kyi theg pa chen po mngon par rtogs pa zhes bya ba'i dkyil 'khor chen po gang du zhugs pas sems can rnams thabs chung ngus de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mchog gi dngos grub thob par 'gyur ba bka' stsal du gsol/ de nas bcom ldan 'das rdo rje rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen pos 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la bka' stsal pa/ 'jam dpal legs so legs so// 'jam dpal khyod gang slar yang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dam tshig la rjes su zhugs pa ni 'jam dpal khyod legs so legs so// de legs par rab tu nyon la yid la zung shig dang theg pa chen po mngon par rtogs pa zhes bya ba'i dkyil 'khor chen po bshad par bya'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das rdo rje rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rjes byin gyis rlob pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas dam tshig chen po rdo rjes byin gyis rlob pa theg pa chen po'i mngon par rtogs pa zhes bya ba'i dkyil 'khor 'di bka' stsal pa/ de nas dkyil 'khor chen po mchog // yang dag rab tu bshad bya ba// dam tshig pha rol tu phyin pa dang / smon lam gyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang / ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang / stobs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang / thabs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang / thams cad kyi pha ro// dpung mgo zlum pa ste yongs su zlum pa'i mgrin pa can du 'gyur ro// thal gong rgyas pa ste/ 'di'i nye bar rgyas par 'gyur zhing gser shog bzhin du rnam par gsal ba'i mgrin pa can no// yan lag so 'tshal ba bzhi yis mngon par dgyes par mdzad do// sangs rgyas kun khyod la phyag 'tshal// chos kyi sku yi mchog gi mchog // gdod ma'i sngags kyi don nyid la// rdo rje ye shes stobs chen la// shin tu sgrib med zhi ba la// rdo rje chos rnams legs gnas pa// theg pa chen po'i go 'phang thob// thugs rje'i bdag nyid can gyi lha// gdod nas dag pa dpa' bo che// dbang phyug dam pa mchog gi mchog // dam chos mchog tu 'gyur ba med// bde gshegs de rnams la phyag 'tshal// zhes pa'o// na ma stu te/ oM mA~M hU~M hU~M na mo stu te swA hA/ 'di ni brjod pa tsam zhig gis// sangs rgyas thams cad rab mchod pa'o// zhes pa'o// // de nas bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad chen pos de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad bos nas 'di skad ces gsungs so// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnams thams cad dngos grub thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor bskyed par mdzad du gsol/ de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnams thams cad slar yang 'dus pa mdzad nas/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje rnal 'byor can gyi dbang phyug chen po la gsol ba btab pa/ bcom ldan 'das khyod nyid kyis rigs thams cad 'khor lo bskyed par mdzad du gsol/ de nas bcom ldan 'das rdo rje rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen pos gsol ba btab pa'i gsung gis de ma thag kho nar 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la bos te bka' stsal pa/ 'jam dpal de bzhin gshegs pa rnams thams cad kyi byang chub kyi snying po nyon cig // ces te/ de nas 'di las yang dag bshad// byang chub dkyil 'khor bla na med// rdo rje ye shes gsang ba mchog // sangs rgyas skyob pa thams cad kyi'o// dben pa'i sa gzhi nyams dga' ba// me tog phreng bas rnam brgyan pa// kun tu sna tshogs cha bzang ba// kun tu sna tshogs sdom par ni// kun nas sna tshogs bya ba rnams// dam pa'i don du bsgrub par bya// ri yi mchog gam grong khyer ni// me tog 'bras bus rnam brgyan pa// der gnas sngags pas dngos grub mchog // gal te 'dod na yang dag bri// gtsug lag khang dang dgon pa'i gnas// ri stengs rnams su kun nas ni// sangs rgyas kun gyi bya ba rnams// dam pa'i don du bsgrub par bya// ma mo'i gnas dang zhi ba'i gnas// dur khrod lha yi gnas su ni// rdo rje 'dzin dpal bya ba rnams// don dam par ni bsgrub par bya// pad+ma'i skyed mos tshal kun dang // chu bo 'dus pa rnams su yang // phyag na pad+ma dpal bya ba// dam pa'i don du bsgrub par bya// rgyal po'i pho brang nyams dga' dang // rgyal po'i skyed tshal rnams su ni// rdo rje rin chen de yi ni// rin chen bya ba rnams bsgrub bya// rtags gcig pa dang ba glang gnas// chu klung 'dus pa rnams su yang // sna tshogs bya ba thams cad rnams// dam pa'i don du bsgrub par bya// dpal ldan rdo rje sems dpa' dang // lha rnams gnas mchog kun tu'o// nam mkha' 'am ni phyogs gzhan du// gang du mnyam par gzhag pa der// rtag pa bsod nams mchog gyur pa// bya ba thams cad bsgrub par bya// phyogs kun mnyam nyid gnas dkyil 'khor// shes rab can gyis thig gdab bya// shar lho nub dang byang rnams kyi// phyogs su dkyil 'khor thig brgyad po// de yi phyi ru 'khor lo ni// kha dog lnga pa cher 'bar ba'o// gru bzhi pa la sgo bzhi pa// rta babs bzhi yis mdzes pa ste// sna tshogs gos dang me tog phreng // rnga yab sogs kyis rnam brgyan pa// dkyil 'khor kun la gnas pa yi// sgo dang sgo khyud mtshams rnams su// rdo rje rin chen rnams kyis spras// dkyil 'khor thams cad bri bar bya// dkyil 'khor de yi dbus su ni// gal te dngos grub mchog 'dod na// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas pa// sangs rgyas gzugs brnyan bri bar bya// shar du bcom ldan 'khor lo can// rdo rje sems dpa' yang dag ldan// 'khor los sgyur ba thams cad ni// sgeg par bcas pa kun bri bya// lho ru gtsug tor dkar po ni// rin chen 'bar ba yang dag ldan// gtsug tor dkar po'i ngos su ni// rdo rje gzi brjid la sogs bri// byang du brtson 'grus chen po ni// gzi brjid phung po stobs po che// sna tshogs rdo rje sogs bcas pa// rim pa kun nas bri bar bya// rdo rje rnal 'byor can gyis ni// dbang phyug mgon po'i nub phyogs su// gtsug tor rgyal ba brtson 'grus che// rdo rje chos sogs dang bcas pa// thams cad sngags pas bri bar bya// gal te dngos grub mchog 'dod na'o// dbang ldan phyogs su 'phags pa gnas// me mtshams su ni cher 'phags so// bden bral du ni rnam rgyal nyid// rlung du de bzhin rnam 'phro ba'o// rdo rje sems dpa' sems dpa' che// sems dpa' kun gyi mdun du ni// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor dbus gnas pa// gsal zhing 'bar 'khrigs 'od zer can// mkhas pas dkyil 'khor rnams su ni// mchod pa rnams ni gzhag byas te// sgeg mo la sogs mchod pa che// de bzhin gzugs sgra la sogs dang // bdug pa la sogs gsang chen no// sgo skyong ba ni bzhi yin te// phyi yi dkyil 'khor gnas rnams su// kun tu bzang po sogs rnams bri// de ltar dkyil 'khor bri bya ste// mchod pa byas nas snga ma bzhin// de bzhin 'jug pa sogs byas la// sgrub pa'i thabs ni brtsam par bya// rdo rje rnal 'byor dbang phyug sogs// dkyil 'khor mngon sum mthong ba las// snga ma rtag pa ji bzhin du// phyi nas de bzhin bri bar bya// bsod nams ji bzhin dkyil 'khor rnams// thams cad mtshon gyis rab brtags pa// rang gi lhag pa'i lha ngo bos// dkyil 'khor thams cad bri byar 'gyur// rang lha'i bdag nyid rnal 'byor gyis// dkyil 'khor thams cad rab tu grub// cho ga dman dang lhag pas kyang // 'grub par 'gyur te skyon ma min// kun tu sna tshogs skal bzang ba// kun nas sna tshogs 'khor lo can// 'khor los sgyur ba bdag nyid che// rin chen bdun gyi mchod pa che// yongs su rdzogs pa'i zla ba ltar// dkyil 'khor bdud rtsi 'byung shes bya// sangs rgyas rdo rje 'dzin sogs kyi// dkyil 'khor 'di ni bshad byas pa'o// phyag na pad+ma bdag nyid che'i// pad+ma'i rnam par rtag shes bya// rin po che yi rin chen rnams// dkyil 'khor sna tshogs rnam pa'o// dkyil 'khor dman zhing dam tshig rnams// dor bar byas pa de nyid ni// gsang ba shes pa ma yin na// sgrub pa'i thabs ni 'grub mi 'gyur// de phyir 'bad pa thams cad kyis// dkyil 'khor thams cad lta ba ni// gal te dngos grub mchog 'dod na// gdon mi za bar rtag tu bya// bla ma la ni yon phul nas// rjes su rim pas bsgrub par bya// brtan pa'am ni g.yo ba yi// rdzas rnams ji snyed thams cad de// rtsa ba me tog 'bras bu sogs// bu mo legs par brgyan byas dang // 'dod pa'i chung ma phul byas nas// slar yang rin gyis bslu bar bya// grong dang de bzhin gtsug lag khang // kun dga' ra sogs rgyal srid mchog // gang la sbyin bya cung zad yod// 'tsho ba de ni sbyin par bya// bdag gi dngos po yongs gtong ba// sangs rgyas thams cad rab mchod pa'o// bla ma la ni yon phul nas// gsang ba dam pa rmad byung ba// mngon par dbang bskur de nas bya// 'dab ma brgyad pa yid 'ong la// slob ma gzhag nas yan lag kun// phyag rgya kun nas bcings byas nas// khams kun rang bzhin rtsa ba dang // sa bon 'bras bus dud pa yi// bum pa rnams kyis dbang bskur te// sangs rgyas phreng ba'i dbang bskur las// spyi bo dang ni dpral ba dang // gzhogs dang de bzhin rgyab tu yang // sangs rgyas rin chen chen po kun// cod pan mchog tu mi 'gyur ba'o// dpal ldan sangs rgyas gtsug nor bu// gdugs dkar steng na gnas pa'o// rgyal srid kun gyi dbang bskur gyis// yang dang yang du dbang bskur bya// dpal kun gyis ni mngon mtho ba// zhes bya'i dbang bskur bshad pa'o// khams kun rang bzhin glang po dang // rta ni mchog tu 'bar ba'am// seng ge'i gdan gnas dbang bskur ba// dpal gyi sngags ni rjod byed cing // dpal gyis mngon mtho zhes bya ba'i// dam pa'i don gyi dbang bskur ba// bkra shis sam ni dpal be'u// gang yang bris nas dbang bskur bya// sangs rgyas dpa' bo thams cad kyis// rnam rgyal dbang bskur zhes bshad do// tsan+dan chu dang bum pa che// gzhan gyis mi thub sman blugs pa// kun nas dbang bskur ched du ni// rtag tu shes rab can gyis brtag // gzhan gyis mi thub dbang bskur mchog // dkyil 'khor gang gang bris byas nas// phyag rgya gang dang gang bkod pa// der ni de dang de brtag bya// de rnams phyag rgya dam par bshad// dbang bskur ched du sangs rgyas rnams// lha de rnams ni yid du 'ong // sman gyi dam pa mchog gyur pa// sangs rgyas kun gyis rab tu bshad// tsan+dan dang ni rgya spos dang // ga pur de bzhin gur gum dang // a ka ru dang lha yi shing // tsan+dan dmar po nyid dang ni// siM hA byA g+h+ri de bzhin mchog // kun nas sa ha de ba dang // gi ri kar+Na tshangs mchod sbyin// sman gyi dam pa rnams su bshad// lhag gnas kun gyi sbyor ba yis// sangs rgyas mchod pa rab 'jug cing // dang po rdo rje dbang bskur ba// shes rab thams cad rab 'jug byed// rin chen dam pa'i dam pa ni// gser la sogs kyis thams cad nas// sman kun dang ni sa bon kun// 'bru rnams thams cad bzang po ni// sangs rgyas byin brlabs rnal 'byor las// dbang bskur don du rab brtag bya// sangs rgyas kun gyi rnal 'byor che// dbang bskur dam pa 'od 'bar ba'o// sangs rgyas kun nas sangs rgyas 'gyur// zhes pa'o// dpal rdo rje snying po rgyan gyi rgyud du ji ltar rnyed pa yongs su rdzogs so// // rigs gzugs skal mang thos blo 'byor sogs// phun tshogs ldan pa dpal ldan chos rje yis// rgyud 'di bsgyur las cung zad ma rdzogs pa// dpal ldan blo gros brtan pas rdzogs par bsgyur//
